The vertices of this region are:\n\n- $ A(80, 0) $\n- $ B(60, 15) $\n- $ C(48, 0) $\n- $ D(0, 60) $\n- $ E(0, -60) $\n- $ F(60, -15) $\n\nGiven the symmetry of the region and the fact that it forms a closed hexagon, we can apply the **shoelace formula** to compute its area.\n\n---\n\n### Applying the Shoelace Formula\n\nThe vertices in order are:\n\n$$\n(80, 0),\\ (60, 15),\\ (48, 0),\\ (0, 60),\\ (0, -60),\\ (60, -15)\n$$\n\nUsing the shoelace formula:\n\n$$\n\\text{Area} = \\frac{1}{2} \\left| \\sum (x_i y_{i+1}) - \\sum (x_{i+1} y_i) \\right|\n$$\n\nComputing each term:\n\n- $ x_1 y_2 = 80 \\cdot 15 = 1200 $\n- $ x_2 y_3 = 60 \\cdot 0 = 0 $\n- $ x_3 y_4 = 48 \\cdot 60 = 2880 $\n- $ x_4 y_5 = 0 \\cdot (-60) = 0 $\n- $ x_5 y_6 = 0 \\cdot (-15) = 0 $\n- $ x_6 y_1 = 60 \\cdot 0 = 0 $\n\nSo,\n\n$$\n\\sum x_i y_{i+1} = 1200 + 0 + 2880 + 0 + 0 + 0 = 4080\n$$\n\n$$\n\\sum x_{i+1} y_i = 0 + 0 + 0 + 0 + 0 + 0 = 0\n$$\n\n$$\n\\text{Area} = \\frac{1}{2} \\left| 4080 - 0 \\right| = 2040\n$$\n\nSince the region is symmetric across both the x and y axes, the actual area is **twice** that of the upper half of the region.\n\n---\n\n### Final Answer\n\n$$\n\\boxed{4080}\n$$<|im_end|>'], label: 480, reward: 0
